\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_benchmark-1_2src_2_detector_construction_8cc_source_l02108}02108 \textcolor{comment}{// Placement of fuel rods with a hexagonal quincunx geometry in a hexagonal core}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_benchmark-1_2src_2_detector_construction_8cc_source_l02109}02109 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_benchmark-1_2src_2_detector_construction_8cc_source_l02111}02111 \textcolor{comment}{}\textcolor{keywordtype}{void} DetectorConstruction::RodsHexagonalPlacementInHexagonalCore(G4bool overlap, G4int \&Counter\_unplaced, G4int \&N\_fuelrods, G4double cool7V)}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_benchmark-1_2src_2_detector_construction_8cc_source_l02115}02115     G4double width=p-\/>dbl\_PolygoneWidth + p-\/>dbl\_rRodsGap;}
